  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_2ffdcb42-167b-4931-867c-234874f541c4'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }

<div id="review_2619055899" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2619055899" />
    <a title="♥ℂĦℝΪՖƬΪℕÅ" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/52207144"><img alt="♥ℂĦℝΪՖƬΪℕÅ" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1568965358p2/52207144.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2619055899?book_show_action=true">Dec 07, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="♥ℂĦℝΪՖƬΪℕÅ" class="user" itemprop="url" name="♥ℂĦℝΪՖƬΪℕÅ" href="/user/show/52207144">♥ℂĦℝΪՖƬΪℕÅ</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52207144?shelf=dystopia-and-utopian">dystopia-and-utopian</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52207144?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52207144?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52207144?shelf=2018-reading-challenge">2018-reading-challenge</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52207144?shelf=novellas">novellas</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52207144?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2619055899" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15355060975844776987"><u>5 Here and Now ★'s</u> <br/><br/><b>
  <i>“It hurt to think of his lips on mine, of all the possibilities he's whispered to me in darkened rooms. He felt so real, so possible.”</i>
</b><br/><br/><i>The Maid</i> is in Lucy's POV (America's maid) and it takes place during <i>The One</i> when they are all on the plane heading back to the palace after visiting with America's family and Maxon calls them all back two days early because he's finally ready to end The selection and pick his Princess :) <br/><br/>This was a very short story. Only 11 pages... and in </span>
  <span id="freeText15355060975844776987" style="display:none"><u>5 Here and Now ★'s</u> <br><br><b>
  <i>“It hurt to think of his lips on mine, of all the possibilities he's whispered to me in darkened rooms. He felt so real, so possible.”</i>
</b><br><br><i>The Maid</i> is in Lucy's POV (America's maid) and it takes place during <i>The One</i> when they are all on the plane heading back to the palace after visiting with America's family and Maxon calls them all back two days early because he's finally ready to end The selection and pick his Princess :) <br><br>This was a very short story. Only 11 pages... and in just that amount of time, I had fallen in love with it! I can't believe it actually brought tears to my eyes 😭 (I'll post the quote that did me in). It seriously made my heart soar with happiness and admiration. I love getting a look into Lucy and Aspen's relationship and I am so happy that they ended up together. Lucy was always my favorite of the maids. As for Aspen, I have always adored and respected him. Whereas Lucy was fragile and quite Aspen was strong and brave. Aspen was Lucy's knight in shining armor and she really needed someone like him in her life. Aspen gave her the strength she needed to come out of her shell and gave her hopes and dreams beyond anything she'd ever allow herself to wish for. Really though this was one of the best couplings and I would love to have an actual book of there story. This just wasn't enough to sustain my needs for more! <br><br>This was such a sweet and tender story about unexpected love and I truly enjoyed getting a bit more on one of my favorite pairings. There love for one another is true and beautiful. This was to damn short in my opinion but it was a strong one! <br><br><u>(This is the quote that made me tear up)</u><br><br><b>
  <i>“Everyday you say something or do something that challenges me, changes me.” “You think you walk, Lucy? I think you fly. You see yourself in a uniform? I see you in a cape. You're a hero, of the quietest but most genuine nature.”</i>
</b><br><br>Illustration of Lucy &amp; How I picture she'd look.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1544184151i/26707645._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <i>“I love you, Aspen. I know it more solidly than I know anything else.”</i>
</b><br><br>Illustration of Aspen &amp; How I picture he'd look.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1544216981i/26711522._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <i>“It took years for her to have that effect on me. It took weeks for you.”</i>
</b><br><br>Merged review:<br><br>Overall these were all really charming and such cute short stories. They were wonderful and really refreshing reads. They were fast-passed and made me smile :) Some much more than others. I loved reading from the different point of views and I am so so happy that I took the time to read this. Each story brought a little something special to the table. Also though very simple, the illustrations are lovely and a great addition. I really liked looking at the map as well. I recommend this to ALL fans of <i>The Selection</i> series! You will not be disappointed. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1543275640i/26652408._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>꧁Individual ratings and reviews of each story below꧂</b><br><br><b>
  <u>THE PRINCE:</u>
</b> ★★★<br><br><b>
  <i>“There was something about her.. Even the way she didn't like me drew me in, and I couldn't help but smile.”</i>
</b> <br><br>This one was just alright for me. I didn't love it but I can't say I hated it either. It's written in Prince Maxon's POV which was initially what drew me in. It takes place a couple of weeks before <i>The Selection</i> which is on his 19th birthday. I really enjoyed the first few chapters. The ones that took place before. It was nice seeing all the preparations for the 'lottery' that wasn't a lottery at all! It was wonderful to be inside Maxon's head, to see his fears and doubts throughout the whole prosses and what his expectations were going into it and whether or not if he'd find love in the end. I have loved Maxon from day one and this just helped solidify it even more. He's charming, sweet, passionate, a bit sheltered and he generally cares about the selection and each one of the girls. I also enjoyed having his thoughts on the girls as well. Especially the one he has about America :) Maxon is so easy to love! The last couple of chapters were retellings of Maxon and America's first few encounters in <i>The Selection</i> just through Maxon's eyes instead. They were pretty boring because it was basically the same. It does give us some good insights though. <br><br>Illustration of Maxon &amp; What I picture he'd look like.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1544255458i/26713496.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1543275640i/26652408._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <u>THE GUARD:</u>
</b> ★★★<br><br><b>
  <i>“Accepting help is its own kind of strength”</i>
</b> <br><br>Again... This was just an okay read. Aspen's POV really didn't add all that much to the story. Shame because I was looking most forward to his. I was hoping for something more sadly this just didn't deliver. On the other hand, it was nice getting a look into his thoughts and feelings and his desires. Aspens POV gives us insight into King Clarkson's nature, motivations, manipulative ways, and his cruelty. I liked getting to see the relationship's form between him and America's maids Anne, Mary and Lucy and the respect they have for him and see the love they have for America. It was nice seeing Aspen's camaraderie with the other guards. Also, I enjoyed the couple scenes between Aspen and the old man who works in the stables. The old man gives some pretty good advice too :) My rating for this story has nothing to do with my liking or not liking Aspen. It's solely based on the content and the entertainment factor which was low in my opinion. And... For the record, I have always loved Aspen ever since the first book! Not necessarily with America but his dedication to America remains steadfast throughout EVERYTHING and he's caring, sweet and all around a wonderful person.<br><br>Illustration of Aspen &amp; What I picture he'd look like.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1544243935i/26712472.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1543275640i/26652408._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <u>THE QUEEN:</u>
</b> ★★★★<br><br><b>
  <i>“You will be the only thing in this world that is truly mine. And I will put you on a pedestal so high, it will be impossible for anyone not to adore you.”</i>
</b> <br><br>This was surprisingly a very delightful read. It's in Amberly's POV and takes place during her very own Selection with Clarkson. For the record, I have never liked Clarkson. He was always portrayed as a mean hurtful tyrant in the first 3 books therefore so my dislike for him lingers in this. Amerly is such a sweet and caring person, though if you've read all the other books then you already know this about her. I didn't love the fact that she was so submissive, whatever he told her to do she would jump. But ya know whatever if it worked for them then so be it. Amberly got what shes always wanted- Clarkson and a whole new life. And Clarkson got a little peace of mind. I do believe their love for one another is genuine at least :) I loved getting a chance to see how Maxon's parents met, I just wish I knew why Clarkson went from this kind-ish guy to be such a hateful man. <br><br>Illustration of Queen Amberly &amp; What I picture she'd look like.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1544336606i/26717771._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Illustration of King Clarkson &amp; What I picture he'd look like.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1544350328i/26718323.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1543275640i/26652408._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <u>THR FAVORITE:</u>
</b> ★★★★★<br><br><b>
  <i>“I’d rather have my last memory be of his death than suffer knowing that his last memory was of mine.”</i>
</b> <br><br>Wow! This was really fantastic!! I gotta say this is my favorite. This is in Marlee's POV and we get a look into Marlee and Carter's relationship, how they first met, how they fell in love and what happened to them after the caning. I love all the extra juicy details into there relationship and I really enjoyed seeing a few scenes that happened throughout <i>The Selection</i> series but through Marlee's eyes. I have been dying to see what exactly led up to that intense and heartbreaking moment that tore at my heartstrings in The Elite and this did not disappoint whatsoever! <br><br>I have adored Marlee from day one when America met her on the plane on there way to the palace in The Selection. In which they became fast friends. Marlee is such an amazing character and I absolutely love her!! So to have this story and in her POV I was beyond thrilled. I love Marlee and America's friendship and I admire her relationship with Carter it melted my heart. Marlee and Carter's relationship was so beautiful and touching and the love they have for one another was so inspiring. I love that even with EVERYTHING... all that they suffered and endured they still managed to persevere. And that ending was everything I had hoped it would be and so much more :)<br><br>Illustration of Marlee &amp; What I picture she'd look like.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1544259268i/26713677.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Illustration of Carter &amp; What I picture he'd look like.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1544396051i/26720593.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1543275640i/26652408._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <u>SCENES FROM CELESTE:</u>
</b> ★★★★<br><br><i>
  <b>“For the first time maybe ever, it didn't matter if I looked beautiful or not. I felt it.”</b>
</i> <br><br>Scenes from Celeste are just that. Three different short scenes from Celestes Perspective. Which includes The Arrival (meeting America, Marlee, and Ashley), The Kiss (Celeste trying to seduce Maxon) and The Departure (leaving the selection). <br><br>I really despised Celeste throughout <i>The Selection</i> series but she won me over in <i>The One</i>. Celeste was the main villain in <i>The Selection</i> series and I gotta admit I loved hating her... but I loved getting to love her even more. I just wish she would have realized all her errors much sooner than she did because I would have loved to have more time with her. In <i>The Selection</i>, we meet this mean, manipulative and vindictive girl who was there for all the WRONG reasons. But once she realizes all her stupid petting mistakes we get to see a whole other side to her. We get to see her vulnerability and kindness and her chance at redemption. She turns out to be such a wonderfully sweet person and an even better friend to America. The ending to <i>The One</i> seriously Broke. My. Heart! <br><br>Scenes from Celeste gives us a better understanding of her actions and I really loved being inside of her head even though they were extremely too damn short! I would have loved having so so much more :) <br><br><b>Illustration of Celeste &amp; How I picture she'd look like.</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1544243935i/26712473.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1543275640i/26652408._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <u>THE MAID:</u>
</b> ★★★★★<br><br><i>
  <b>“It hurt to think of his lips on mine, of all the possibilities he's whispered to me in darkened rooms. He felt so real, so possible.”</b>
</i> <br><br>The Maid is in Lucy's POV (America's maid) and it takes place during <i>The One</i> when they are all on the plane heading back to the palace after visiting with America's family and Maxon calls them all back two days early because he's finally ready to end <i>The Selection</i> and pick his Princess :) <br><br>I fell in love with this! I can't believe it actually brought tears to my eyes 😭. It seriously made my heart soar with happiness and admiration. I loved getting a look into Lucy and Aspen's relationship and I am so happy that they ended up together. Lucy was always my favorite out of the maids. As for Aspen, I have always adored and respected him. Whereas Lucy was fragile and quite Aspen was strong and brave. Aspen was Lucy's knight in shining armor and she really needed someone like him in her life. Aspen gave her the strength she needed to come out of her shell and gave her hopes and dreams beyond anything she'd ever allow herself to wish for. This was one of the best couplings and I would love to have an actual book of there story. This was such a sweet and tender story about unexpected love and I truly enjoyed it. There love for one another is true and beautiful. This was such a strong addition! I WANT MORE!!! <br><br><i>
  <b>“Everyday you say something or do something that challenges me, changes me.” “You think you walk, Lucy? I think you fly. You see yourself in a uniform? I see you in a cape. You're a hero, of the quietest but most genuine nature.”</b>
</i> <br><br>Illustration of Lucy &amp; What I picture she'd look like.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1544243935i/26712474.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1543275640i/26652408._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <u>THE EPILOUGE:</u>
</b> ★★★<br><br><i>
  <b>“I knew we were only just getting to the best part of our lives.”</b>
</i> <br><br>The Epilogue is another really short story which is in America's POV. It takes place two years after The Selection has ended and it's on Maxons birthday. <br><br>I didn't really have a strong connection with <i>The Epilogue</i>. It felt a bit rushed and I think for something like this it would have benefited from being a little longer. For what this was though I did still enjoy it and I'm glad I took the couple minutes it took to read it. It was very sweet and I loved getting to see little glimpses of the friendship that has formed between Maxon and Aspen and I liked seeing a little bit of May and that Marlee and Carter have a one-year-old son named Kile. But it did kinda feel like it was just tossed in there. I also love that it took place on Maxons birthday. America throws him a party and has such a wonderful surprise in store for him at the end.<br><br>Illustration of Maxon &amp; America and what I picture they'd look like.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1544485688i/26724583.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1543275640i/26652408._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <u>WHERE ARE THEY NOW?:</u>
</b> ★★★<br><br>I guess this was a nice way to wrap up the series. <i>WHERE ARE THEY NOW?</i> shows us what happens to Kriss, Natalie, and Elise after they left the Selection. It was nice getting a little more background on them, but I really wasn't a fan of the way the story was told. It all felt really rushed and I wish it would have gone into a little more depth but they're all doing pretty much what you'd expect. I felt the saddest for Kriss because she had it the hardest time after but I'm truly happy she and the other two girls eventually found there HEA's as well :) I probably would have enjoyed this much more if <i>Kiera Cass</i> wrote from their perspective. That being said it was a quick and easy read-only containing 11 pages so I figured I might as well read it. This was really a bittersweet moment for me! <br><br>What I picture Kirss, Natalie and Elise would look like. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1544251723i/26712731._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="15355060975844776987" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1435782991" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1435782991" />
    <a title="Jennifer" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2473504-jennifer"><img alt="Jennifer" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1394406877p2/2473504.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1435782991?book_show_action=true">Nov 06, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer" href="/user/show/2473504-jennifer">Jennifer</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2473504-jennifer?shelf=read-2015">read-2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2473504-jennifer?shelf=short-stories-and-novellas">short-stories-and-novellas</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2473504-jennifer?shelf=young-adult-genre">young-adult-genre</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2473504-jennifer?shelf=listened-to-audiobook">listened-to-audiobook</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2473504-jennifer?shelf=companion-novel">companion-novel</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2473504-jennifer?shelf=dystopia">dystopia</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1435782991" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18085243147782262097">Not sure why I thought this was going to be another installment in the series. Just a heads up...it's not. <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/24465724.Happily_Ever_After__The_Selection___0_4__0_5__2_5__2_6_' title='Happily Ever After (The Selection, #0.4, 0.5, 2.5, 2.6) by Kiera Cass' rel='nofollow noopener'>Happily Ever After</a> is a compilation of all the novellas and bonus scenes/epilogues in <u>The Selection</u> series and if you are up-to-date with reading the series then you have already read most of these. Die hard fans will likely love this one-stop shop for all the extras but I could have done without it. Don't mind me, just a little disgruntled. I should have read the synopsis first. Lesson lea</span>
  <span id="freeText18085243147782262097" style="display:none">Not sure why I thought this was going to be another installment in the series. Just a heads up...it's not. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/24465724.Happily_Ever_After__The_Selection___0_4__0_5__2_5__2_6_" title="Happily Ever After (The Selection, #0.4, 0.5, 2.5, 2.6) by Kiera Cass" rel="nofollow noopener">Happily Ever After</a> is a compilation of all the novellas and bonus scenes/epilogues in <u>The Selection</u> series and if you are up-to-date with reading the series then you have already read most of these. Die hard fans will likely love this one-stop shop for all the extras but I could have done without it. Don't mind me, just a little disgruntled. I should have read the synopsis first. Lesson learned.<br><br><b><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15820748.The_Prince__The_Selection___0_5_" title="The Prince (The Selection, #0.5) by Kiera Cass" rel="nofollow noopener">The Prince</a> (with the two bonus chapters):</b><br>Review from July 2013:<br>★★★★☆<br>Novella #0.5. This is basically the first 1/3 of The Selection from Prince Maxon's point of view. I liked that it showed the stressors Maxon has to deal with, his relationship with his parents, and his personal thoughts about the selection process and the girls.<br><br><b><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18170039.The_Guard__The_Selection___2_5_" title="The Guard (The Selection, #2.5) by Kiera Cass" rel="nofollow noopener">The Guard</a>:</b><br>Review from March 2014:<br>★★★☆☆<br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18170039.The_Guard__The_Selection___2_5_" title="The Guard (The Selection, #2.5) by Kiera Cass" rel="nofollow noopener">The Guard</a> is a novella (#2.5) in author <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2987125.Kiera_Cass" title="Kiera Cass" rel="nofollow noopener">Kiera Cass</a>'s The Selection series. In the series, the female lead is America Singer who is torn between two loves in her life, Maxon and Aspen. Maxon's perspective is shared in the novella <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15820748.The_Prince__The_Selection___0_5_" title="The Prince (The Selection, #0.5) by Kiera Cass" rel="nofollow noopener">The Prince</a>, and Aspen's perspective is shared in this novella. I have enjoyed the series overall and although I thought <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15820748.The_Prince__The_Selection___0_5_" title="The Prince (The Selection, #0.5) by Kiera Cass" rel="nofollow noopener">The Prince</a> novella was unnecessary, it was interesting being inside Maxon's head. However, after reading <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18170039.The_Guard__The_Selection___2_5_" title="The Guard (The Selection, #2.5) by Kiera Cass" rel="nofollow noopener">The Guard</a>, I almost wish I wasn't exposed to Aspen's point-of-view. There's a difference between a man being in love and a boy being in love and Aspen appears to be the latter. There's nothing necessarily wrong with this. Actually, there's a certain type of sweetness to being oblivious to everything except your heart's desire. But America is no longer a girl who has this luxury. She has grown and has been exposed to the complexities in her world and her eyes are now on more pressing matters. I've been Team Maxon since book one and that hasn't changed for me, especially after reading this book.<br><br><b><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22054340.The_Queen__The_Selection___0_4_" title="The Queen (The Selection, #0.4) by Kiera Cass" rel="nofollow noopener">The Queen</a>:</b><br>Review from March 2015:<br>★★★★☆<br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22054340.The_Queen__The_Selection___0_4_" title="The Queen (The Selection, #0.4) by Kiera Cass" rel="nofollow noopener">The Queen</a> is a prequel novella (#0.4) in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2987125.Kiera_Cass" title="Kiera Cass" rel="nofollow noopener">Kiera Cass</a>'s young adult, dystopian series titled: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18735913.The_Selection_Series_Boxed_Set_The_Selection___The_Elite___The_Prince__The_Selection___0_5__1_2_" title="The Selection Series Boxed Set The Selection / The Elite / The Prince (The Selection, #0.5, 1-2) by Kiera Cass" rel="nofollow noopener">The Selection Series</a>. This short story features Maxon's father and mother, King Clarkson and Queen Amberly, and includes the story of how they met through their generation's selection process. <br><br>I think most readers don't like King Clarkson in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18735913.The_Selection_Series_Boxed_Set_The_Selection___The_Elite___The_Prince__The_Selection___0_5__1_2_" title="The Selection Series Boxed Set The Selection / The Elite / The Prince (The Selection, #0.5, 1-2) by Kiera Cass" rel="nofollow noopener">The Selection Series</a>, so I was curious if he would be portrayed any differently during his younger years as prince. <br><br>The answer is...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1425437096ra/13889759.gif" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I have to admit though, Ms. Cass was much more subtle in her character development of Clarkson, but his need to control and his hard-handed threats are still shown through his interactions with others in this prequel. The cycle of violence rings loud and clear within the portrait of this royal family, but any suggestion that Clarkson is a victim rang on deaf ears with me. Amberly is the perfect little submissive, which is something I didn't really view her as in the series, but maybe I just forgot. Through Amberly's point of view, the two of them have a very promising future together, and they may very well be just what each other needs. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22054340.The_Queen__The_Selection___0_4_" title="The Queen (The Selection, #0.4) by Kiera Cass" rel="nofollow noopener">The Queen</a> gives quite a bit of insight into these two characters, and when compared to the series, does a great job of reinforcing the fairytale aspect of Maxon and America's love story. This novella is a wonderful addition to the series and I would recommend it to fans.<br><br><b><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22917292.The_Favorite__The_Selection___2_6_" title="The Favorite (The Selection, #2.6) by Kiera Cass" rel="nofollow noopener">The Favorite</a>:</b><br>★★★☆☆<br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22917292.The_Favorite__The_Selection___2_6_" title="The Favorite (The Selection, #2.6) by Kiera Cass" rel="nofollow noopener">The Favorite</a> is a novella (#2.6) in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2987125.Kiera_Cass" title="Kiera Cass" rel="nofollow noopener">Kiera Cass</a>'s young adult, dystopia series titled <u>The Selection</u>. This short-story was a refreshing addition from Marlee's point of view. The characters in this series are great, but sometimes it's nice to read a new perspective...and see a new love story. If you have read the series then you know that Marlee falls in love with a guard: Carter and when discovered, they are caned as punishment. But Marlee's POV provides insight into a beautiful bond between two people that gets them through the hard times. I found the novella rather choppy and it didn't flow well in my opinion but the content was good. Three stars.<br><br><b>Three scenes from Celeste’s POV:</b><br>★★★☆☆<br>Wow, so Celeste isn't the cold-hearted b*itch I thought she was. She's still a stuck-up snob who will do anything to be first but she is a bit complex like we all are. Can't say I like her character but I didn't mind reading these few scenes from her perspective.<br><br><b>Lucy’s scene (bonus scene from The One):</b><br>★★☆☆☆<br>This is a tiny little scene from the maid Lucy's perspective. If this was a deleted scene collecting dust, then I see why Ms. Cass wanted to eventually offer it to readers but I certainly wouldn't have sought out <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/24465724.Happily_Ever_After__The_Selection___0_4__0_5__2_5__2_6_" title="Happily Ever After (The Selection, #0.4, 0.5, 2.5, 2.6) by Kiera Cass" rel="nofollow noopener">Happily Ever After</a> just for this.<br><br><b>The bonus epilogue:</b><br>★★☆☆☆<br>Another tiny piece that gives fans a peek of their favorite characters' after the ending of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18635016.The_One__The_Selection___3_" title="The One (The Selection, #3) by Kiera Cass" rel="nofollow noopener">The One</a>. Again, it didn't really do anything for me but I'm sure there are some fans out there that will just squeal with joy at any little bit that extends the story for them.</span>
  <a data-text-id="18085243147782262097" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2132001913" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16307819898224293111">I'm so happy to have finally read this!! Huge shout-out to Rizoli for lending it to me, by the way. This made me remember why I love Kiera Cass' writing so much. It's because I don't have to think at all and because it is so addictive. It took me so little time to read even though I'm so busy in school! It was also nice to be back in this world and the feels hit me hard with the pictures and the happiness and I just... I feel happy. </span>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1241289356" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1241289356" />
    <a title="Muse-ic ♬" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/36574090-muse-ic"><img alt="Muse-ic ♬" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1497741975p2/36574090.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1241289356?book_show_action=true">Mar 30, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Muse-ic ♬" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Muse-ic ♬" href="/user/show/36574090-muse-ic">Muse-ic ♬</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36574090-muse-ic?shelf=novella-short-story">novella-short-story</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36574090-muse-ic?shelf=dystopian">dystopian</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36574090-muse-ic?shelf=royalty-celebrities-or-rich-people">royalty-celebrities-or-rich-people</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1241289356" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4439767052904880812">I'm not covering this review for spoilers. Just be warned that there will be spoilers for <i>The One</i>.<br/><br/>That was a lovely read!<br/>Mostly................<br/><br/><b>The Prince</b><br/>I miss Maxon. He is definitely in the list of my top five book boyfriends. I've already read <i>The Prince</i>, but this one had two extra chapters. LOVED 'EM!!<br/>♥<br/><br/><b>The Guard</b><br/>Let's be honest here. I don't like Aspen. So I skimmed through <i>The Guard</i>. I read Lucy's POV that include Laspen (Lucy/Aspen).<br/>I'm not going to lie: I feel bad for Lucy. Aspen was kind o</span>
  <span id="freeText4439767052904880812" style="display:none">I'm not covering this review for spoilers. Just be warned that there will be spoilers for <i>The One</i>.<br /><br />That was a lovely read!<br />Mostly................<br /><br /><b>The Prince</b><br />I miss Maxon. He is definitely in the list of my top five book boyfriends. I've already read <i>The Prince</i>, but this one had two extra chapters. LOVED 'EM!!<br />♥<br /><br /><b>The Guard</b><br />Let's be honest here. I don't like Aspen. So I skimmed through <i>The Guard</i>. I read Lucy's POV that include Laspen (Lucy/Aspen).<br />I'm not going to lie: I feel bad for Lucy. Aspen was kind of a jerk. Not like a mean jerk, but Lucy asked him if he still had feelings for America and such and he told her that "no" but his instinct to protect her would always be there. It makes sense, but that comment really hurt Lucy. She told him to leave her alone, but he didn't. It worked out in the end, but I still wasn't feeling it.<br /><br /><b>The Queen</b><br />I didn't even bother to reread this. I read it already and lost respect for Amberly and hated Clarkson even more. I just skipped over it.<br /><br /><b>The Favorite</b><br />I loved <i>The Favorite</i>. It was great to find out how Marlee met Carter and what happened to them after their beating. Awesome!<br /><br /><br /><b>Lucy's Chapters</b><br />As mentioned above.<br /><br /><b>Three Scenes from Celeste's POV</b><br />Holy Crap! I miss Celeste. These scenes made me miss her more. I loved reading them!<br /><br /><b>The Bonus Epilogue</b><br />I've already read this, but I read it again just because. Awesome and adorable!<br /><br /><b>Where are they now?</b><br />This was a follow-up of Natalie, Kriss, and Elise (no Celeste because we know where she is now :'( )<br />Natalie's was interesting and made complete sense. She got married, divorced because she's too much of a free spirit, and became a famous jewelry designer.<br />Kriss was so sad. She just went back to teaching at her father's university. Eventually she met Professor Elliot, who was seven years her senior. He didn't treat her like a prior-selected because he was on a research trip away from Illea and never knew about it. They fell in love and got married.<br />Elise was so devastated by her loss that she wouldn't step foot in the palace. She didn't even attend the royal wedding! But once Maxon learned that his father started the war in New Asia for sh*ts and giggles, he took out the troops, made peace, and made Elise the ambassador for New Asia. Then she met an amazing man from New Asia, found love, and married him (not out of duty). They had kids.<br /><br />The whole war in New Asia thing made me hate Clarkson even more. In the One, Queen Amberly told America that Clarkson seemed harsh because he cared and tried so hard and that it was really stressful to be in his shoes. I lost even <i>more</i> respect for Amberly after this. Was she <i>that</i> stupid????<br />Clarkson was evil. Everything he did was for power and for himself, not for the country. It was mentioned that if the Southern Rebels came to power, everything they would do would be for power.....Doesn't sound too different from Clarkson. <b>I hate him from the bottom of my heart!!!</b><br /><br /><br />The illustrations from this book were gorgeous :D I tried to put some in this review but they didn't work unfortunately.<br />If you've read the Selection series, I would definitely recommend reading this as well :D</span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1390304573" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1390304573" />
    <a title="Mikee (ReadWithMikee)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/44137919-mikee-readwithmikee"><img alt="Mikee (ReadWithMikee)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1583262285p2/44137919.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1390304573?book_show_action=true">Sep 12, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mikee (ReadWithMikee)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mikee (ReadWithMikee)" href="/user/show/44137919-mikee-readwithmikee">Mikee (ReadWithMikee)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9780062414083" href="/book/show/24585402-happily-ever-after">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1390304573" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8294026187668070372"><b>Sigh. So many people have complained about this bind-up being a ploy to leech money from its readers, but I DON'T CARE. The cover is beautiful. The illustrations were beautiful. I love the Selection series. Judge away! :P</b><br/><br/>In all honesty, <i>I don't really bother reading novellas.</i> Don't ask me why because I don't know the answer myself haha. I'm probably just too lazy. Or maybe because I would rather read new books with new stories and characters. It better be one <b>HECK</b> of a series for me to even cons</span>
  <span id="freeText8294026187668070372" style="display:none"><b>Sigh. So many people have complained about this bind-up being a ploy to leech money from its readers, but I DON'T CARE. The cover is beautiful. The illustrations were beautiful. I love the Selection series. Judge away! :P</b><br /><br />In all honesty, <i>I don't really bother reading novellas.</i> Don't ask me why because I don't know the answer myself haha. I'm probably just too lazy. Or maybe because I would rather read new books with new stories and characters. It better be one <b>HECK</b> of a series for me to even consider reading a novella. But I decided to purchase this bind-up anyways because as previously said, I LOVE the Selection series. It's actually one of the first series I've read that brought me back to my love for books and reading. So I didn't mind spending money on this beautiful piece of work because I never spent money on the novellas that were released prior to <i>Happily Ever After</i> in the first place.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>With that being said...</i>
</b><br /><br /><b>
  <u>The Queen: 2/5 STARS</u>
</b><br />Sadly, I did not like Queen Amberly's story mainly because I didn't particularly like her character. I never gave Queen Amberly much thought in the original books. I figured she was kind, humble, and loved by her people for good reason. Nothing more to it than that. Instead, the Amberly in this novella was just plain <b>
  <i>weak</i>
</b> in my opinion. She was head over heels in love over a prince she only knew from what she saw on television and hadn't even had a proper conversation with him. She was a complete <b>
  <i>pushover</i>
</b> and would jump if you told her to jump without question. This girl honestly had no backbone and it irritated the living <i>crap</i> out of me. The insta-love felt super cringeworthy and I didn't really connect with any of the characters. The Queen is definitely my <b>
  <i>least favorite</i>
</b> novella from the book.<br /><br /><b>
  <u>The Prince: 4/5 STARS</u>
</b><br />Honestly, this should've been more of a novella during the Selection told in Maxon's POV instead of making Daphne and her unrequited love for Maxon play even the slightest role in the story. She was <i>irrelevant</i> to me and all I really wanted was to finally get to the part where Maxon and America meet. Not to mention the fact that her character was just so <b>annoying and needy.</b> And the <i>"romance"</i>... Ugh. It's so weird. All the newly introduced relationships so far up until this point are so rushed and cringeworthy. I get that these are just novellas and there aren't enough pages for development but <i>ugh.</i> This is why I don't read novellas! But it all got better when Maxon and America finally met. They were just so adorable and just... <b>
  <i>AWWWW!</i>
</b> And Maxon is such a great guy! I loved getting a peek of what his thoughts really were during the Selection. I was so disappointed when the story ended and honestly wouldn't mind it one bit if Kiera rewrote the whole book in Maxon's POV. It was just crazy realizing how much I've missed Maxon and America! &lt;3<br /><br /><b>
  <u>The Guard/The Maid: 3/5 STARS</u>
</b><br />I don't think I really enjoyed this one as much. I love Aspen's character but I felt like I was basically rereading the Elite all over again. I didn't get much out of it as much as I did with The Prince. We spent most of the timing just going over what happened in the original books but never really getting anything new. At least, nothing new that was overly exciting. I wanted to know more about Lucy and Aspen's relationship because their romance <b>
  <i>came out of nowhere</i>
</b> in the One. I had hoped that Kiera would've shed some light on when and how Aspen's <i>"love"</i> for Lucy triumphed over his love for America but I still didn't really see it. They only had about two scenes together in The Guard and they were nothing more than friendly conversation. I wanted to see that moment when Aspen <b>KNEW</b> he loved Lucy. But since we never really got that in The Guard or The Maid, I think I'll always feel that Aspen only ended up with Lucy for the sake of ending up with someone and having a happy ending.<br /><br /><b>
  <u>The Favorite: 5/5 STARS</u>
</b><br />Omg this was by far <b>my favorite</b> novella! I absolutely loved Marlee and Carter. The only complaint I have is that this story was simply not long enough! Even though we couldn't get much development because this story was just a novella, the romance between Marlee and Carter was still perfect. Unlike Aspen and Lucy's "relationship" in The Guard, we actually got to see Marlee and Carter's love <b>
  <i>flourish.</i>
</b> I was definitely sold! Marlee and Carter are my second favorite, if not the only other couple I ship besides America and Maxon. &lt;3<br /><br /><b>
  <u>Celeste: 4/5 STARS</u>
</b><br />I AM STILL UPSET OVER HOW CELESTE'S OVERALL STORY ENDS. I don't think I can ever forgive Kiera for this! I hated Celeste with a burning passion and loved her instantly as soon as she redeemed herself in the end. <b>
  <i>BUT WHY WHY WHY DID YOU HAVE TO RUIN IT!!!</i>
</b> As much as I loved reading Celeste's POVs, it made me even more upset that she didn't get a better ending. <i>Ugh!!!!!</i><br /><br />I still can't believe the Selection is over! :( It just feels so bittersweet to finally see everybody have their <i>
  <b>happily ever after.</b>
</i> I truly believe that Kiera Cass should've ended the series after America and Maxon's story. As much as I want this series to go on forever, it just isn't the same anymore even with the original characters still there. Just let them have their HEA. Let us believe that Illea was finally in a state of peace after everything has happened.</span>
  <a data-text-id="8294026187668070372" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer14853437198237831678">3.5* <br/><br/>I really don’t know how I should properly review this book of short stories...<br/><br/>Well I just wanted to start off by saying that I really like how Kiera Cass gave us a glimpse into the lives of characters so that we could understand them and their motives a little better. <br/><br/>The Queen - I thought this section was very interesting, but Amberly is very naive and the romance was so dry. It’s like one day they met, they next they get married. And also Amberly had no reason to be helplessly in love wit</span>
  <span id="freeText14853437198237831678" style="display:none">3.5* <br /><br />I really don’t know how I should properly review this book of short stories...<br /><br />Well I just wanted to start off by saying that I really like how Kiera Cass gave us a glimpse into the lives of characters so that we could understand them and their motives a little better. <br /><br />The Queen - I thought this section was very interesting, but Amberly is very naive and the romance was so dry. It’s like one day they met, they next they get married. And also Amberly had no reason to be helplessly in love with Clarkson. I also hate how Clarkson chose the girl who listened to him the most...I find that a bit controlling. I wish we got a peek in Clarkson’s head.<br /><br />The Prince - Not that detailed of a review since its parallel to America’s story. I did understand and like Maxon’s character a bit more after this. <br /><br />The Guard - I honestly could care less about this because I know he doesn’t end up with America soooo...<br /><br />The Favorite - I was very excited to read this part because Marlee was such a cute and bubbly character. However, I found this story quite boring. The romance, like with Amberly, was pretty dry. It wasn’t as bad and immediate as Amberly’s, but it wasn’t what I was hoping for. <br /><br />Scenes from Celeste - This, I really enjoyed. It was interesting to be in the head of the mean girl who develops so much throughout the series. <br /><br />The Maid - Wow, this was a definite behind the scenes story. You realize that Aspen was kind of cheating on America even though it didn’t seem like that from America’s point of view for sure. <br /><br />Where are they now? - I could honestly care less where they are lol. I was just interested in the people who still have connections with America. </span>

<div id="review_2602145603" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2602145603" />

      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title=" " href="/book/show/28245673-scenes-from-celeste">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52207144?shelf=novellas">novellas</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52207144?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52207144?shelf=2018-reading-challenge">2018-reading-challenge</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2602145603" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11435420344835365226"><u>4 I didn't need a Man ★'s</u> <br/><br/><b>
  <i>“For the first time maybe ever, it didn't matter if I looked beautiful or not. I felt it.”</i>
</b><br/><br/><i>Scenes from Celeste</i> are just that. Three different short scenes from Celestes Perspective. Which includes <i>The Arrival</i> (meeting America, Marlee and Ashley), <i>The Kiss</i> (Celeste tryng to seduce Maxon) and <i>The Departure</i> (leaving the selection). <br/><br/>Oh boy, I really despised Celeste throughout <i>The Selection</i> series but she won me over in <i>The One</i>. Celeste was the main villain in <i>The Select</i></span>
  <span id="freeText11435420344835365226" style="display:none"><u>4 I didn't need a Man ★'s</u> <br><br><b>
  <i>“For the first time maybe ever, it didn't matter if I looked beautiful or not. I felt it.”</i>
</b><br><br><i>Scenes from Celeste</i> are just that. Three different short scenes from Celestes Perspective. Which includes <i>The Arrival</i> (meeting America, Marlee and Ashley), <i>The Kiss</i> (Celeste tryng to seduce Maxon) and <i>The Departure</i> (leaving the selection). <br><br>Oh boy, I really despised Celeste throughout <i>The Selection</i> series but she won me over in <i>The One</i>. Celeste was the main villain in <i>The Selection</i> series and I gotta admit I loved hating her... but I loved getting to love her even more. I just wish she would have realized all her errors much sooner than she did because I would have loved to have so much more from her. In <i>The Selection</i> we meet this mean, manipulative, vindictive, bitter girl who was there for all the WRONG reasons. But once she realizes all her stupid petting mistakes we get to see a whole other side to her. We get to see her vulnerability and kindness and her chance at redemption. She turns out to be such a wonderfully sweet person and an even better friend to America. I love getting to see Celeste grow out of it and the ending to <i>The One</i> seriously Broke. My. Heart! <br><br>Anyways, <i>Scenes from Celeste</i> gives us a better understanding of her actions and I really loved being inside of her head even though they were extremely too damn short! I would have loved having so so much more. I recommend this to all <i>The Selection</i> fans out there :) <br><br>Illustration of Celeste &amp; How I picture she'd look. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1544171110i/26706832._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer15298429464090428643">While I wouldn't rate every story in this collection 4 stars, it was interesting to garner an insight into the other characters from The Selection series and further my understanding of their motives and actions. I found some parts a little repetitive as alot of the scenes were featured in the main series but viewing them from an alternate perspective was fascinating. Also, knowing the ending of each story did not impact my enjoyment of them, as I thought it might. I love an author who takes the</span>
  <span id="freeText15298429464090428643" style="display:none">While I wouldn't rate every story in this collection 4 stars, it was interesting to garner an insight into the other characters from The Selection series and further my understanding of their motives and actions. I found some parts a little repetitive as alot of the scenes were featured in the main series but viewing them from an alternate perspective was fascinating. Also, knowing the ending of each story did not impact my enjoyment of them, as I thought it might. I love an author who takes the time to expand their fictional worlds in this way so this collection combined is wholly deserving of 4 stars.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer8444030351243138540"><i>Out of all the books I've read in The Selection series, this is definitely my favorite! (Although it's not another installment, just a compilation of novellas) In this book, you'll have a clearer view of every character and somehow understand their decisions throughout the story. My personal favorites are The Favorite and After The One. <b>At first, I had my doubts about this series, but I found myself loving every part of it!</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1469173086i/19787602._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>Quotable Quotes</b><br/><blockquote>"I could feel my dreams slipping through my fingers. I mig</blockquote></i></span>
  <span id="freeText8444030351243138540" style="display:none"><i>Out of all the books I've read in The Selection series, this is definitely my favorite! (Although it's not another installment, just a compilation of novellas) In this book, you'll have a clearer view of every character and somehow understand their decisions throughout the story. My personal favorites are The Favorite and After The One. <b>At first, I had my doubts about this series, but I found myself loving every part of it!</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1469173086i/19787602._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>Quotable Quotes</b><br><blockquote>"I could feel my dreams slipping through my fingers. I might as well embrace defeat now. It would hurt less later."<br>"I liked it here, in his arms. I'd always wondered what they'd feel like."<br>"It's a strange thing to discover how much you matter to people you didn't really know you mattered to."<br>"His world looked like a storm. I was going to be its center."<br>"This was joy. This was love. So many words you hear about or read about, and now... now I knew them."<br>"You will be the only thing in this world that is truly mine."<br>"Any girl who would risk her life for someone she loves certainly deserves to be called a lady."<br>"I'd studied her face in a dozen shades of light, in a thousand stolen moments. With her words, I knew without a doubt: she loved me."<br>"But I've seen a lot of people let the bad around them make them hard or stubborn. In the end, they miss the chance to make their world better because they only see the worst in it."<br>"She seemed paralyzed now, afraid of taking any kind of step because she didn't know what would fall apart along the way."<br>"Yes, we still had a long way to go, but I knew it wouldn't feel that way if we were in it together."<br>"I want her to stay. It seems like everyone leaves when I need them to stay."<br>"We know you're strong, but accepting help is its own kind of strength."<br>"And I just thought that maybe I could give you a shot at a life that would be better than the one that I would have been able to give you. And I convinced myself that was the right way to love you."<br>"You're the only thing I've ever wanted to fight for."<br>"He was control to her chaos; she was levity to his seriousness."<br>"Maybe you stole me. Because I distinctly remember belonging to myself once, but now I'm all yours."<br>"I needed to be beside him tonight. So much was going through my head, and I knew he was my only safe place."<br>"Love only yourself a little bit longer, until you can't stand not to love someone else."<br>"So that's the only kind of love I've ever understood. When you love someone, you sacrifice."</blockquote></i></span>

    <a title="Lauren Lanz" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/82987361-lauren-lanz"><img alt="Lauren Lanz" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1586150400p2/82987361.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2786254770?book_show_action=true">Apr 14, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lauren Lanz" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lauren Lanz" href="/user/show/82987361-lauren-lanz">Lauren Lanz</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/82987361-lauren-lanz?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/82987361-lauren-lanz?shelf=novellas">novellas</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/82987361-lauren-lanz?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/82987361-lauren-lanz?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/82987361-lauren-lanz?shelf=4-stars">4-stars</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2786254770" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2251234942344128164">This collection of novellas was basically the dessert that no one needs, but we take it anyways because it’s damn good.<br/><br/>I’m going to review this novella by novella because that’s just the sophisticated trash I am.<br/><br/><b>The Queen: ★★★★★<br/>The Prince: ★★★★<br/>The Guard: ★★★★★<br/>The Favourite: ★★★★★<br/>Scenes From Celeste: ★★<br/>The Maid: ★★★★<br/>After The One: ★★★★<br/>Where are They Now?: ★★★<br/></b><br/><br/><b>The Queen</b><br/><br/>Amberly’s backstory -when taken into account with her marriage in The Selection- was quite tragic. Then Kiera Cass had the <i>audacity</i></span>
  <span id="freeText2251234942344128164" style="display:none">This collection of novellas was basically the dessert that no one needs, but we take it anyways because it’s damn good.<br /><br />I’m going to review this novella by novella because that’s just the sophisticated trash I am.<br /><br /><b>The Queen: ★★★★★<br />The Prince: ★★★★<br />The Guard: ★★★★★<br />The Favourite: ★★★★★<br />Scenes From Celeste: ★★<br />The Maid: ★★★★<br />After The One: ★★★★<br />Where are They Now?: ★★★<br /></b><br /><br /><b>The Queen</b><br /><br />Amberly’s backstory -when taken into account with her marriage in The Selection- was quite tragic. Then Kiera Cass had the <i>audacity</i> to go and slaughter me by adding pieces of foreshadowing to this novella. Hinting at what happened in The One. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[In this novella, one of the selected girls asked Amberly if she would take a bullet for Clarkson, in which Amberly figured it would never happen, and said yes <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />Getting a glimpse into her love for Clarkson was sweet. The way that I interpreted things, it was clear that they both cared for one another, even if Amberly and Clarkson refused to acknowledge the obvious faults in their relationship.<br /><br />Love is blind, that much was clear with Amberly. It’s unfortunate the way that things turned out for them in future years.<br /><br /><b>The Prince</b><br /><br />I actually smiled typing out <i>The Prince</i> for some reason, which should be tell enough as to how I felt about this novella. Maxon is the sweetest of sweet, and getting to see the way he perceived the Selection during the earlier stages was great. <br /><br />Amberly never fails to demonstrate what an amazing mother she is. Getting more of her admirable qualities and love for her son is always welcome with me.<br /><br />I liked how Kiera gave us a small look at Maxon’s relationship with Daphne, as I was left slightly curious once finishing The One, not expecting to get any further information on her. Especially after America asked about her in the selection, getting that extra little bit of backstory was great.<br /><br />And Maxon’s first impression of America- *breathes* -everything.<br /><br /><b>The Guard</b><br /><br />I’m currently near tears, having just finished The Guard. The first thing I thought after reading the last sentence of this novella was <i>Oh, Aspen.</i> Everyone in the fandom seems to hate on Aspen for his actions in The Elite, but any lingering hate or doubt in my mind was eliminated after getting to see his thoughts.<br /><br />The Guard is a glimpse into the selection through Aspen’s eyes. His thought process and feelings for America were definitely irritating when viewed from her perspective in the main series. Reading from Aspen’s mind really hit me.<br /><br />It made me realize that I never really had a reason to dislike Aspen. He’s actually quite sweet in this novella, I feel stupid for missing any of this personality in the main series.<br /><br />Aspen is wonderful to the maids, treating them like the good friends he’s become to them all. <br /><br />One of my favourite things about this novella was Aspen’s bromance with Avery and the rest of the palace guards. It’s funny how even occupation can form the strongest of bonds between people. It was nice to know that during his time serving as a palace guard, Aspen was in good company, even if he didn’t have much time to spend with his new guard buddies.<br /><br />Anyone who’s read this novella will know what had me near tears the last two pages. This resulted from the words Aspen spoke to America while she was asleep.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“I couldn’t save my dad. I couldn’t protect Jemmy. I can barely keep my family afloat, and I just thought that maybe I could give you a shot at a life that would be better than the one that I would have been able to give you. And I convinced myself that was the right way to love you.”</i>
</b><br /><br />Aspen pushed America to join the selection in hopes that she would find a better life than he would have been able to provide for her. That’s real love right there, and suddenly I don’t know how myself or anyone else ever hated Aspen.<br /><br />Aspen might have just become my favourite character of the series. This novella flipped my entire view of him.<br /><br /><b>The Favourite</b><br /><br />Marlee’s love story was probably one of the most pure I’ve read. Both her and Carter obviously hold a devotion to each other that is beyond words.<br /><br />The little flashbacks to how Marlee and Carter discovered each other were perfect. I wasn’t expecting a story on Marlee in the first place, and I didn’t realize we needed it so much. Getting to see that she got a happy end after all was amazing. I’m glad that Kiera felt the need to elaborate on her story, because it was well appreciated and very much needed to give Marlee some closure.<br /><br /><b>Scenes from Celeste</b><br /><br /><br />This novella felt almost pointless to me. My opinions of Celeste haven’t changed much, but if anything, the first two parts to this only made her seem far more self-absorbed than The Selection made her out to be.<br /><br />This novella made me realize that if Maxon wasn’t smart enough to realize that Celeste was putting on an act, she might as well have won the entire thing, stringing him along for nothing but the crown.<br /><br /><b>The Maid</b><br /><br />Here’s the final verdict: Aspen is my new favourite of this series. I feel like these novellas have opened us up to a whole other side of Aspen that was missing in The Selection. <br /><br />Lucy is so sweet, her relationship with America was always pleasing to follow, and seeing her get a happy ending in The Maid was lovely.<br /><br />Aspen and Lucy bonding over their hardships was tough for me to take. I ship them so much, and I’m really glad to see that things worked out for them. Absolutely wonderful novella.<br /><br /><b>After The One</b><br /><br />*unintelligible screaming*<br /><br /><b>Where are They Now?</b><br /><br />My favourite thing about this novella, and also the only thing worth noting, was the fact that Kriss and her husband are raising exotic pets instead of children. That thought pus a smile to my face every time.<br />------------<br /><br />Surprisingly, when I calculated the average of my ratings for each novella in this book, it came out to be exactly 4 stars. I would say that some of the novellas in here were so good I enjoyed them more than the main series, though there were others I didn’t find necessary or like nearly as much.<br /><br />Regardless, I’ve given all three main books of The Selection 4 stars as well. <br />I guess math wants to leave me undecided.</span>
  <a data-text-id="2251234942344128164" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

The Queen<br/>Okay this kinda broke my heart to see how Amberley ignored all the signs of his character (including his proposal!!!!!) purely because she was in love with him and thought that he was tr</span>
  <span id="freeText5687093512955095232" style="display:none">3.5⭐️<br /><br />The selection series is such an easy/chill read 100% recommend for something light hearted &lt;3<br /><br />This novella is really worth reading it gave the plot so much more depth :)<br />The book is split up into essentially 8 parts so I have individual reviews ⤵️⤵️⤵️<br />⚠️spoilers if you haven’t read the other books⚠️<br /><br /><br />1. The Queen<br />Okay this kinda broke my heart to see how Amberley ignored all the signs of his character (including his proposal!!!!!) purely because she was in love with him and thought that he was truly a good person :((<br />And how Clarkson only really liked her because she submissive and didn’t challenge him and maybe wanted to take his anger out from his controlling parents, by in turn controlling her and Maxon which is just so sick I-<br /><br />2. The Prince <br />READING THE START OF THE SELECTION FROM MAXONS POINT OF VIEW WAS EVERYTHING😭😭<br />It was the funniest and sweetest thing it was my favourite out of the novellas :)<br />I also thought it was quite notable how Amberley talks about how any girl putting her name in the selection would want a way out of quiet, and how when America talks about how it was a mistake etc. it could partly be why Maxon was initially drawn to her, because she wasn’t seeking to get away from the quiet Maxon longed for.<br />it also linked to the ‘After the One’ where he has a big party but is completely happy which crosses how he was in the party in the beginning of The Prince, because he has America and friends he loves 🥺<br /><br />3. The Guard <br />Aspens point of view was kinda interesting to see how he perceived everything, he’s honestly so sweet :)<br />I also loved the small developments in his and Lucy’s relationship<br /><br />4. The Favourite <br />Marlee and Carter’s story was really well done, with the going back and forth between the canning and their falling for each other :)<br />Seeing what Marlee thought about Maxon and America and just her general point of view from the scenes was the sweetest thing, and how Maxon’s roll in helping them was more developed<br /><br />5. Scenes from Celeste <br />It was really an effort not to cry at her scenes, especially when she talks about her future and I really wish that I could have read about her making real friends, and developing her friendship with America :(<br />She was just becoming a good person by recognising her flaws, and fixing them and it just really ✨hurt✨<br /><br />6. The Maid<br />Aspen and Lucy deserved each other in the best possible way and I’m so glad that I got to read more about their relationship :)<br /><br />7. After The One<br />I SAW WHAT WAS COMING IN THIS AND IT WAS EVERYTHING 🥺<br />“Let it fall to pieces. So long as I have my America in my arms.”<br />Seriously do they get cuter I stg 😩<br /><br />8. Where are they now?<br />awh I’m so happy that they all found ways to fufill themselves :)</span>

<div id="review_1278503575" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1278503575" />
    <a title="Drew" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/22104588-drew"><img alt="Drew" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1498412758p2/22104588.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1278503575?book_show_action=true">May 12, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Drew" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Drew" href="/user/show/22104588-drew">Drew</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9780062414083" href="/book/show/24585402-happily-ever-after">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22104588-drew?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22104588-drew?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1278503575" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5935956634073241105">I don't know if <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22918050.The_Heir__The_Selection___4_' title='The Heir (The Selection, #4) by Kiera Cass' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Heir</a> ruined this series for me or I'm just outgrowing these books, but this collection of Selection novellas wasn't as enjoyable as I expected it to be.<br/><br/>I've always thought of Kiera Cass's books as addicting, cheesy, and lots of fun. That's why I always come back to them because I know I can finish them in a day and get a couple hours of entertainment out of them.<br/><br/>I never noticed these books were <b>so cheesy they were unrealistic,</b> though, and the characters weren't as lovable as </span>
  <span id="freeText5935956634073241105" style="display:none">I don't know if <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22918050.The_Heir__The_Selection___4_" title="The Heir (The Selection, #4) by Kiera Cass" rel="nofollow noopener">The Heir</a> ruined this series for me or I'm just outgrowing these books, but this collection of Selection novellas wasn't as enjoyable as I expected it to be.<br><br>I've always thought of Kiera Cass's books as addicting, cheesy, and lots of fun. That's why I always come back to them because I know I can finish them in a day and get a couple hours of entertainment out of them.<br><br>I never noticed these books were <b>so cheesy they were unrealistic,</b> though, and the characters weren't as lovable as I remembered them to be. I didn't feel much excitement from reading about a young Queen Amberly and Aspen and Lucy's turmoil really wasn't that emotional.<br><br>I used to think the romance in Cass's books was the sweetest, swooniest, most romantic thing in the world. But I found the romance in this collection bland and with not much chemistry going on. <b>The couples were too <i>perfect</i> to be believable.</b> They were like that annoyingly flawless couple whom you can never understand.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1448747318i/17183259.jpg" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I didn't buy Marlee and Carter's romance. Marlee tripped, Carter carried her to the hospital, they exchanged a few words, and we were supposed to believe they were in love? Their banter wasn't even cutesy or funny, let alone romantic.<br><br>Celeste's chapters were my favorite. I loved the short scenes from her point of view. Kiera did a surprisingly well job of creating a believable, cruel, pitiless mean girl. But she also explained Celeste's side of things. She wasn't heartless, she was just putting on a show and doing whatever it took to win the crown. She <i>knew</i> she would make a good queen and was determined to gain that position.<br><br>I skipped over the stories <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15820748.The_Prince__The_Selection___0_5_" title="The Prince (The Selection, #0.5) by Kiera Cass" rel="nofollow noopener">The Prince</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18170039.The_Guard__The_Selection___2_5_" title="The Guard (The Selection, #2.5) by Kiera Cass" rel="nofollow noopener">The Guard</a> because I had already read them. To be fair, I remember liking them a lot, and I liked the addition of pretty illustrations.<br><br>I don't know if Kiera is becoming sloppier with writing romance, I just know that I invested every ounce of my fangirling heart in the love story between America, Maxon, and Aspen, but with Kiera's newest book, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22918050.The_Heir__The_Selection___4_" title="The Heir (The Selection, #4) by Kiera Cass" rel="nofollow noopener">The Heir</a>, and now this collection of romance-filled novellas, I'm finding the romance quite dry.<br><br>Oh well. There's always <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/25817407.The_Siren" title="The Siren by Kiera Cass" rel="nofollow noopener">The Siren</a> to look forward to.</span>
  <a data-text-id="5935956634073241105" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1545244573?book_show_action=true">Feb 11, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Luzie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Luzie" href="/user/show/42006839-luzie">Luzie</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>
