        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1545244573" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8221622731360186235">I really enjoyed the concept of this book!<br/>The Queen was the first novella in the book, and it showed the romatic pairing of Queen Amberly (in her perspective) and King Clarkson. The love between them was so well, necessary in some way that still showed they found there true soulmate. Amberly is a calm and willing women which provides for her family perfectly fine. She was the one true queen of Illèa!<br/>The Prince i have read before. It was fun reading it again. Maxon`s perspective should have been </span>
  <span id="freeText8221622731360186235" style="display:none">I really enjoyed the concept of this book!<br />The Queen was the first novella in the book, and it showed the romatic pairing of Queen Amberly (in her perspective) and King Clarkson. The love between them was so well, necessary in some way that still showed they found there true soulmate. Amberly is a calm and willing women which provides for her family perfectly fine. She was the one true queen of Illèa!<br />The Prince i have read before. It was fun reading it again. Maxon`s perspective should have been longer but the intensity of the story gave it such a good content. Though some characters *cough*Daphne*cough* were kind of annoying.<br />The Guard was kind of too long. I know we all love Aspen despite his threat to America`s and Maxon`s love but i kind of thought his perspective was dull and protracted. His devoteness towards America i think it almost borders to obsession. <br />The Favorite was a sweet novel explaining the circumstances that true love and worthship has to endure before their happy ending. I think even though Marlee did experience luxury, the first ever happy moment she shared was with Carter and that made the novella that much sweeter.<br />The extras at the end gave the book a slight nodge up, especially yhe "After The One" scene which was probably my most loved scene in this book.<br />4/5 stars</span>

<div id="review_1434893981" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1434893981" />
    <a title="ashleigh" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/45502331-ashleigh"><img alt="ashleigh" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1598153155p2/45502331.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1434893981?book_show_action=true">May 29, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="ashleigh" class="user" itemprop="url" name="ashleigh" href="/user/show/45502331-ashleigh">ashleigh</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1434893981" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3179679715771137077"><b> 3.81/5 </b><br/>this series isn't perfect. it has flaws: the world doesn't make sense, there is some lowkey sexism that really is never addressed or challenged which ew, but the thing is, i have so much fun reading about these characters. that and it can be cute as hellllll. <br/><br/><i>The Queen (4.5/5) </i><br/>To me this was one of the more interesting dynamics in the Selection series. Clarkson is this terrible guy, and then there is Amberley who is the complete opposite. While this relationship is manipulative (from Cla</span>
  <span id="freeText3179679715771137077" style="display:none"><b> 3.81/5 </b><br />this series isn't perfect. it has flaws: the world doesn't make sense, there is some lowkey sexism that really is never addressed or challenged which ew, but the thing is, i have so much fun reading about these characters. that and it can be cute as hellllll. <br /><br /><i>The Queen (4.5/5) </i><br />To me this was one of the more interesting dynamics in the Selection series. Clarkson is this terrible guy, and then there is Amberley who is the complete opposite. While this relationship is manipulative (from Clarkson) and lowkey obsessive (on Amberley's part) I really liked reading about it. I really enjoyed that peek into Clarkson's life and to actually learn more about him as a character. I would have even liked an entire novel on the two of them. <br /><br /><i>The Prince (3/5) </i><br />I read this before when it was first released as an e-book. While I can't help but be a little smitten with Maxon, he did kind of annoy me in this? He is just so aloof, you kind of begin to question his position. It's cool though cus I think this highlights the development he goes through in the series. It was cute tho.<br /><br /><i>The Guard (2/5)</i><br />I really cannot stand Aspen. I liked having a look into the life as a guard, but that was about it? He is possessive and all he does is talk about america. He also has this superiority complex and just...nah fam. I don't like him and I never will #sorrynotsorry. He’s not even interesting? Clarkson is shit and I hate him, but at least he’s got a bit of intrigue.<br /><br /><i>The Favourite (5/5) </i> <br />This was lowkey repetitive sometimes, but I don't care. I love me some romance and this delivered. I love Carter and Marlee. My heart hurt for them, but the way they care about each other has me crying in the club fearing that I'm going to die alone. <br /><br /><i>Scenes from Celeste (5/5) </i><br />This mah bitch and I love her. My one true queen tbh.<br /><br /><i>The Maid (3.5/5) </i><br />I like Lucy a lot so hearing from her was fun. I feel like we are often presented with a version of a strong character, and Lucy has her own kind of strength. She chooses to fight but she's quieter, softer. This wasn't my favorite, but homegirl stood her ground so props.<br /><br /><i>After the One (5/5) </i><br />I'm allergic to children but this was sofuckingcute!!!!!!<br /><br /><i>Where are they Now? (2.5/5)</i><br />This was kind of unnecessary. I'm glad Kriss got some dope ass pets tho.</span>
  <a data-text-id="3179679715771137077" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('6NuFoDZxJAAaPYFR3fPfE+XviLz24KPIERRGVAP7MLBQ4sZ1bcffAKDfMiVEj333n3azwy3FwFViGIJmKJvHcQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('KMSXB+rZD5V5xeIIb+RAycSTeTdd6erXs1eJF+XCBLKQ/dTSsW/0lcMnUXz2mOItvgpCSIbMiUrAW00lzqLzcw==')})
  }
